neghboure thou shalt couet thy neghbours housse nether shalt couet thy neghbours wife servaunte mayde oxe asse oughte people sawe thunder ad thethe avve causeth vvrath ad maketh fle god gospell clawes therfore vnclene swyne though deuyde hoffe two clawes yet cheweth cud ad therfore vnclene flesh see ye eate ad carkasses se ye twych vnclene shall ye eate water soeuer hath finnes skales water made heer white ad rawe flesh sore also olde leprosye skynne flesh preast shall make vnclene ad shall shutte vp vnclene yf leprosye breake skynne couer skynne heed fote ouer wheresoeuer preast loketh let preast loke apon yf leprosye haue couered flesh let make disease clene moch altogether white therfore cleane yf rawe flesh sene shalbe vn cleane therfore preast seeth rawe flesh let make vnclene moch flesh rawe vnclene suerly true leprosye yf rawe flesh departe agayne chaunge vnto white let come preast let preast se yf sore chaunged vnto white let preast make disease cleane ad cleane byele vncleane leprosye broken place byele yf preast loketh white heeres therein nether scabbe lower skynne somwhat blackesh preast shall shutt aparte vij dayes yf sprede abrode meane season let preast make talked moses saynge speake vnto childern israel ad saye vnto lorde youre god wherfore doynges land egipte wherein ye dwelt se ye doo nether doynges lande canaan whether bringe nether walke ye ordinaunces doo iudgeme te kepe myne ordynaunces walke therein lorde youre god kepe therfore myne ordinaunces ad iudgemetes whiche yf man doo shall lyue thereby lorde se ye goo none youre nyghest kyn red vncouer secrettes lorde secrettes thy father thy mother se thou vnheale thy mother therfore shalt thou discouer hir secrettes secrettes thy father wife shalt thou discouer thy father secrettes thou shalt discouer preuyte thy syster doughter thy father thy mother whether borne home without thou shalt discouer secrettes thy sonnes doughter thy doughters doughter thyne awne preuyte thou shalt discouer secrettes thy father wyues doughter bare thy father thy suster thou shalt therfore discouer hir secrettes thou shalt vncouer secrettes thy father syster thy father nexte kyn thou shalt dyscouer secrettes thy mother syster thy mother nexte kyn thou shalt open secrettes thy father brother thou shalt goo wife thyne awnte thou shalt discouer secrettes thy doughter lawe thy sonnes wyfe therfore vncouer hir secrettes thou shalt vnheale secrettes thy brother wife thy brother preuyte thou shalt discouer preuytes wife ad hir doughter also nether shalt thou take hir sonnes doughter hir doughters doughter vncouer secrettes hir nexte kyn therfore wikydnesse thou shalt take wife hir sister vexe hir thou woldest open hir secrettes longe lyueth thou shalt goo vnto woman open hir secrettes longe put aparte hir vnclennesse thou shalt lye thy neghbours wife defyle thi selfe thou shalt geue thi seed offer vnto moloch thou defile name thi god lorde thou shalt lye mankynde womankynde abominacion thou shalt lye maner beeste defile thy selfe therewith nether shall woman stonde beest lye doune thereto abhominacion defile youreselues thinges thinges nacions defiled whiche cast lande defiled visett wykednesse thereof apon lande shal spe hir inhabiters kepe ye therfore myne ordinaunces iudgementes se ye commytt none abominacions nether ony straunger soiourneth amonge abhominacions haue men lande done whiche lande defiled lest lande spewe ye haue defiled spewed nacions whosoeuer shall comytt abhominacions soules commytt shall perish amonge people therfore se ye kepe myne ordinaunces ye commytt none abhominable customes commytted ye defile youre selues therewith lorde youre god p xix chapter lorde spake vnto moses sayenge speake vnto multitude childern israel iudgementes ye shulde kepe lorde p xx chapter lorde talked moses saynge tell childern israel whosoeuer childern israel straungers dwel israel geueth seed vnto moloch shall dye people lande shall stone hi stone wil sett face apon felowe destroye amonge people hath geuen seed vnto moloch de file sanctuary polute myne holy name though people landeif transgr esse god commaundemetes may happelye escape ordlye iudges ca avoid firse wrath god wil surely find v hyde eye felowe geueth seed vnto moloch kyll yet put face apon man apon houssholde destroy goo whooringe co mytt hoordome moloch amonge people yf soule turne vnto worke spirites maker dysemall dayes goo whoorynge wilt put face apon soule destroye amonge people sanctifie youre selues therfore holye lorde youre god se ye kepe myne ordinaunces doo lorde sanctifie whosoeuer curseth father mother shall dye bloude heed hath cursed father mother breaketh wedlocke another man wife shall dye hath broke wedlocke neghbours wife shall likewise yf man lye father wife ad vncouer father secrettes shall dye bloude apon heedes yf man lye doughter lawe thei shall dye haue wrought abhominacion bloud vpon heedes yf man lye mankynde maner woma kynd haue co mitted abhominacion shall dye bloude apon heed yf man take wife ad hir mother thereto wekednesse shall burne fire wekednesse amonge yf man lye beest shall dye ye shall slee beest yf woma go damsell vowe vowe vnto lorde binde herselfe beynge hir father housse vnmaried yf hir father heare hir vowe bonde hath made vppon hir soule holde pea thereto hir vowes bodes hath made vppo hir soule shall stonde effecte yf hir father byd daye heareth none hir vowes bondes hath made vppon hir soule shalbe value ad lorde shall forgeue hir father forbade yf husbonde vowed pronounsed oughte hir lippes wherewith bonde hir soule hir husbonde de helde peace daye herde hir vowes hir bondes wherewith bounde hir soule shal stonde effecte ad yf hir husbonde forbade daye herde hath made hir vowe vppo none effecte also whiche pronounsed hir lippes wherewith bounde hir soule lorde shall forgeue vowe wedowe deuorsed haue bound soules shall stonde effecte yf vowed husbandes housse bounde soule oth husbande herde helde peace forbade vowes bondes wherewith bound soule shall sto de yf husbande disanulled daye herde nothing proceded lippes vowes ad boundes wherewith bounde soule shall stonde effecte husbande hath lowsed lorde shall forgeue vowes othes binde humble soule maye husbande stablish breake yf husbande hold peace one daye vnto another stablisheth vowes boundes whiche vppon helde nought quyckely wekednesse thyne invencyons thou hast forsaken lorde lorde shall make pestilence cleaue vnto vntyll haue consumed londe whether thou goest enioye lorde shall smyte swellynge feuers heet burnynge wetherynge smytynge bia stinge shall folowe vntyll thou perishe heauen ouer thy heed shalbe b asse erth vnder yerne lorde shall turne rayne la de vnto powder ad dust euen fro heauen shal come doune vpo vntyll thou brought nought lorde shall plage thine enemyes thou shalt come one waye agenst flee seuen wayes ad shalt scatered amonge kingdomes erth thy car casse shalbe meate vnto maner foules ayre ad vnto beestes erth man shall fraye awaye lorde smyte botch egipte morodes scalle maungynesse thou shalt healed thereof lorde shall smyte madnesse blyndnesse dasynge herte thou shalt grope none daye blynde gropeth darkenesse shalt come right waye thou shalt suffre wronge polled euermore man shall soker thou shalt betrothed vnto wife another shall lye thou shalt bylde housse another shall dwell therein thou shalt plante vyneyarde shalt make comen thine oxe shalbe slayne thyne eye ad thou shalt eate thereof thine asse shalbe violently taken awaye euen thi face shall restored agayne thy shepe shalbe geuen vnto thine enemyes ad man shall helpe thy sonnes ad thy doughters shall geue vnto another nacion thyne eye shall se dase vppon daye longe shalt haue myghte thyne hande frute thy londe thy laboures shall nacyon thou knowest eate ad thou shalt soffre violence oppressed alwaye thou shalt cleane besyde thy selfe syghte thyne eye whiche thou shalt se lord shall smyte myscheuous botche knee ad legges thou ast healed eue sole fote vnto toppe heed lorde shall brynge thy kynge thou hast sett ouer vnto nacyon whiche nether thou thy father haue knowne thou shalt serue straunge goddes euen wodd ad stone thou shalt goo wast ad made ensample ad gestynge stocke vnto al nacios whether lord shall carye thou shalt carie moch seed ou felde shalt gather litle locustes
